(medianArray.length % 2) == 1 ) {\n                        medianIndex = medianArray[ (medianArray.length - 1) / 2 ];\n                    } else {\n                        medianIndex = medianArray[ (medianArray.length / 2) - 1 ];\n                    }\n                    \n                }\n                properStatIndices[i] = medianIndex;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        \n        \n        \n        \n        var orderedIndices = [];\n        for ( var i = 0; i < properTopIndices.length; i++) {\n            orderedIndices[i] = i;\n        }\n        if (order == 'median') {\n            orderedIndices.sort(function(a,b){return score_stat[properStatIndices[b]]-score_stat[properStatIndices[a]]});\n        } else { // if (order == 'device') {\n            orderedIndices.sort(function(a,b){return score_top[properTopIndices[b]]-score_top[properTopIndices[a]]});\n        }\n        \n        var ticketMapping = new Array();\n        matchingTicketNumber = 0;\n        for ( var i = 0; i < orderedIndices.length; i++) {\n            matchingTicketNumber++;\n            var showIt = ( matchingTicketNumber <= ((currentPage + 1) * ticketsPerPage) ) && ( ticketMapping[ticketIndex] = orderedIndices[i];\n            }\n        }\n        \n        \n        for (var ticketIndex = 0; ticketIndex < Math.min(ticketsReady, ticketMapping.length );
